## [features]

## Cookie Settings for Exemplary AI

Why We Use Cookies

Exemplary AI leverages cookies to ensure essential functionalities of our enterprise solutions and to elevate your user experience. Choose preferences for each cookie category. To learn more, please read our Privacy Policy.

Essential CookiesEssential Cookies

These cookies are critical for the functionality of Exemplary AI’s services. Without them, our services may not perform optimally.

| Name | Domain | Expiration | Purpose |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| \_\_utmc | exemplary.ai | Session | Typically used for session tracking. |
| \_\_hssrc | exemplary.ai | (not provided) | Typically used to determine if the visitor has restarted their browser. |

Performance and Analytics CookiesPerformance and Analytics Cookies

These cookies help us understand how clients interact with our enterprise solutions, ensuring we continue to provide top-tier offerings.

| Name | Domain | Expiration | Purpose |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| \_ga | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used to distinguish users. |
| \_gcl\_au | exemplary.ai | 1 Day | Used for experimenting with advertisement efficiency. |
| \_clsk | exemplary.ai | 1 Day | Typically used for tracking users interactions. |
| \_\_hssc | exemplary.ai | 1 Day | Used for tracking sessions. |
| \_\_hstc | exemplary.ai | 6 Months | Used for tracking visitors. |
| \_\_utma | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used for distinguishing users and sessions. |
| \_\_utmz | exemplary.ai | 6 Months | Used for tracking traffic sources. |
| ajs\_user\_id | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used for analytics purposes. |
| ajs\_group\_id | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used for analytics purposes. |
| ajs\_anonymous\_id | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used for analytics purposes. |
| muxData | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Typically used for performance analytics. |

Advertisement and Targeting CookiesAdvertisement and Targeting Cookies

These cookies help us tailor marketing efforts and offers to your specific needs, ensuring you receive relevant information.

| Name | Domain | Expiration | Purpose |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| intercom-device-id-vrpp7ymp | exemplary.ai | 9 Months | Typically used for targeted messaging and advertisements. |
| intercom-id-vrpp7ymp | exemplary.ai | 6 Months | Typically used for targeted messaging and advertisements. |
| intercom-session-vrpp7ymp | exemplary.ai | 7 Days | Typically used for targeted messaging and advertisements. |

Need More Information?

For any queries related to our cookie policy or choices, please contact Exemplary AI.

Accept AllReject AllSave Settings

## Automate Your Content Creation Process

Features

### Transform Long Videos to Short Viral Clips Instantly

Repurpose your long videos and create social media ready short clips instantly

![Image](https://exemplary.ai/_next/image?url=%2Fimg%2Flanding%2Ffeatures%2Fhomepage%2Ffeature-1.png&w=1080&q=75&dpl=dpl_6VBeXkRbw6UjjU88xLtQpkjkq7pG)

Features

### Edit Videos Instantly From The Transcript

Instant transcript for your audio/video with >98% accuracy. Easily edit the video from transcript like a doc.

![Image](https://exemplary.ai/_next/image?url=%2Fimg%2Flanding%2Ffeatures%2Fhomepage%2Ffeature-2.png&w=1080&q=75&dpl=dpl_6VBeXkRbw6UjjU88xLtQpkjkq7pG)

Features

Upload your video/audio file or link to Exemplary AI

## 2. Repurpose your Content with AI

## 3. Share and Download

## Cookie Settings for Exemplary AI

Why We Use Cookies

Exemplary AI leverages cookies to ensure essential functionalities of our enterprise solutions and to elevate your user experience. Choose preferences for each cookie category. To learn more, please read our Privacy Policy.

Essential CookiesEssential Cookies

These cookies are critical for the functionality of Exemplary AI’s services. Without them, our services may not perform optimally.

| Name | Domain | Expiration | Purpose |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| \_\_utmc | exemplary.ai | Session | Typically used for session tracking. |
| \_\_hssrc | exemplary.ai | (not provided) | Typically used to determine if the visitor has restarted their browser. |

Performance and Analytics CookiesPerformance and Analytics Cookies

These cookies help us understand how clients interact with our enterprise solutions, ensuring we continue to provide top-tier offerings.

| Name | Domain | Expiration | Purpose |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| \_ga | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used to distinguish users. |
| \_gcl\_au | exemplary.ai | 1 Day | Used for experimenting with advertisement efficiency. |
| \_clsk | exemplary.ai | 1 Day | Typically used for tracking users interactions. |
| \_\_hssc | exemplary.ai | 1 Day | Used for tracking sessions. |
| \_\_hstc | exemplary.ai | 6 Months | Used for tracking visitors. |
| \_\_utma | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used for distinguishing users and sessions. |
| \_\_utmz | exemplary.ai | 6 Months | Used for tracking traffic sources. |
| ajs\_user\_id | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used for analytics purposes. |
| ajs\_group\_id | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used for analytics purposes. |
| ajs\_anonymous\_id | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Used for analytics purposes. |
| muxData | exemplary.ai | 1 Year | Typically used for performance analytics. |

Advertisement and Targeting CookiesAdvertisement and Targeting Cookies

These cookies help us tailor marketing efforts and offers to your specific needs, ensuring you receive relevant information.

| Name | Domain | Expiration | Purpose |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| intercom-device-id-vrpp7ymp | exemplary.ai | 9 Months | Typically used for targeted messaging and advertisements. |
| intercom-id-vrpp7ymp | exemplary.ai | 6 Months | Typically used for targeted messaging and advertisements. |
| intercom-session-vrpp7ymp | exemplary.ai | 7 Days | Typically used for targeted messaging and advertisements. |

# The Complete  ‍ **AI Clipping Platform** ‍

# Built for Brands

Flowjin AI turns branded long videos and audios into clips and writes platform‑specific copy. Just approve and publish across all social platforms.

[Get Short Clips](https://www.flowjin.com/#)

Thank you! Your submission has been received!

Oops! Something went wrong while submitting the form.

or

[Upload](https://app.flowjin.com/auth/register)

Or upload videos after signing up

## **How it Works**

### AI Clips The Most Worthy Moments

AI finds the moments worth sharing in your media files and drafts 6–12 captioned clips automatically.

Your browser does not support the video tag.

### Then AI Writes Platform‑specific Copies

Flowjin writes platform‑specific posts — titles, descriptions, hashtags, and CTAs for LinkedIn, YouTube, and X — ready to tweak and approve.

Your browser does not support the video tag.

### Schedule & Publish Without Leaving The Platform

One‑click scheduling across channels from a single calendar, so the whole week ships in minutes.

Your browser does not support the video tag.

## Who We’re Built For

### Founders & CEOs

Maintain a consistent LinkedIn cadence for your founder brand by having AI cut your long-form content into weeks of clips.

### Marketing Leads

Turn every webinar into a multi‑week, multi‑channel campaign with measurable pipeline impact.

### Social Media Managers

Stay consistently present on all social platforms without juggling tools. We replace your video editor + AI copywriter + social media posting tool.

### Marketing Agencies

Deliver more to clients without hiring more editors. AI clips your videos on-brand, then you review and schedule everything from one calendar.

## One Platform for Video & Audio

### Video → On‑brand clips in minutes

\- Smart crop & speaker tracking

\- Auto captions, titles, and B-rolls

\- Social platform specific copy already written for you

\- Approve and schedule

[**Try it Now**](https://app.flowjin.com/)

### Audio→ Branded soundbites in minutes

\- Podcasts into audiograms and quote clips in minutes

\- AI already writes all social platform‑specific copies

\- One click add to the calendar & publish

[**Try it Now**](https://app.flowjin.com/)

## We've Got the Answers

How does Flowjin work?

1\. Upload or Import Your Video

Bring in your content from YouTube, Apple, or upload directly from your device.

2\. Let Flowjin’s AI Do the Work

Our AI scans your video and automatically generates 10+ short, captioned clips optimized for engagement.

3\. Make It Yours

Customize each clip with your branding, style, and layout to match your voice.

4\. Publish Anywhere

Export your clips to LinkedIn, X, or YouTube— complete with AI-generated captions and descriptions.

What are the most common use cases of Flowjin?

Flowjin automatically generates short videos from long-form content (10+ minutes). Our users leverage Flowjin to transform podcasts, webinars, calls, interviews, and monologues into engaging content for Instagram Reels, YouTube Shorts, TikTok, LinkedIn, and Facebook.

What languages are supported?

We support a wide range of languages such as English, French, Spanish, German, and many more.

How long do you store my videos?

You can access to your project for only up to 30 days after upload. After that, any drafted clips will be deleted but you can always download any clips you exported in Flowjin.

What functionalities does your video editor has? Can I edit the clips afterwards?

Yes, we have a simple but advanced AI-powered video editor. You can trim or extend the clips, customize the captions and the layout, add overlays and build branded templates to apply to all clips later on.

Does Flowjin work with videos shorter than 10 minutes?

Flowjin performs optimally with videos longer than 10 minutes, where it identifies the most compelling moments. However, Flowjin adapts to any uploaded content, intelligently extracting relevant scenes to create engaging clips regardless of length.

## Pricing FAQs

Do you provide captions and transcriptions for video clips?

Yes, we offer the option to include embedded subtitles in your video clips. Additionally, for each video clip, you can choose to download the subtitles and transcriptions separately.

What languages are supported?

Currently we support English, Spanish, Portuguese, French, Dutch, German, Italian media but we plan to add more languages soon.

What's the fastest way to reach you in case I need help?

To contact us, you can email us at [contact@flowjin.com](mailto:contact@flowjin.com), or leave a message on the live chat widget on the Flowjin website.

If I cancel my plan can I get a refund?

No. We don't have a refund policy on all subscription plans and all sales are final. Please check our [Terms of Service](https://www.flowjin.com/terms-of-service) for more details.

Do my credits carry over into the next month?

Yes! Your unused credits from the previous billing period will carry over to the next month. However, rollover credits can only carry over for one month and cannot accumulate further. This feature is available for paid plans (Starter, Creator).

Do projects expire?

Project expiration depends on your plan when you created it: Free plan projects expire after **5 days**, Starter plan expire after **60 days**, and **Creator plan projects never expire**. Once expired, you can still access and download your exported clips, but draft clips will no longer be available for editing. If you need to work on those drafts again, you'll need to re-upload and reanalyze your file, which will use credits from your account.

‍

How do I cancel my subscription?

You can easily cancel your subscription from your Flowjin account. You can also delete your account and permanently wipe your data from our servers.

What does AI Processing Hours mean?

AI Processing Hours is the amount of time our AI will process your media files. The output of processing includes assets repurposed from your media files including video clips, quote images, social copies and more.

We use cookies

This site uses cookies and related technologies, as described in our Privacy Policy for purposes including site operation, analytics, enhanced user experience, and advertising.

[No, thanks](https://www.flowjin.com/pricing#) [It's OK](https://www.flowjin.com/pricing#)

## FAQs

### What is a credit, and how is it charged?

Credits work like currency on our platform and are used for video creation, generative models and across other features, not for downloading content. Generative models are priced differently, All models available at their original API pricing. You can use your credits however you like across the platform. We reserve the right to update credit costs at any time, without prior notice.

Heads up: Unused credits don't roll over to the next month.

AI editing models

## AI that understands every pixel of your video

The most powerful AI editing models that work on any video. Built for speed, accuracy, and creative flexibility.

![ClipAnything](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6388604483b03a9ecb34d695/684c2798958314e4a8958d21_ClipAnything.avif)

### ClipAnything

Every other AI clipping tool only works with video podcasts. ClipAnything is the only AI clipping model that turns any genre — vlogs, gaming, sports, interviews, explainer videos — into viral clips in 1 click.

### ReframeAnything

The only AI reframe model that resizes any video for any platform and keeps moving subjects centered with AI object tracking. If you want more control, use manual tracking to instruct AI exactly what to follow.

Workflow automation

## Your video creation process — now on autopilot

Create and publish videos 5x faster with OpusClip’s web app and API, so you can go on vacation and still keep your content rolling.

![Your video creation process — now on autopilot](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6388604483b03a9ecb34d695/684dbfb6a4157e1095cf61af_workflow.avif)

AI editor

## AI that edits with you, not just for you

Take full editing control, or let our AI take over. Either way, it’s effortless.

OpusClip for teams

## Scale your creative output and business without scaling overhead

Every business is becoming video-first. OpusClip helps your brand stay top of mind.

![Brand templates](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6388604483b03a9ecb34d695/684c306adfce8ae39556b260_Brand%20templates.avif)

### Brand templates

Create various brand templates with on-brand font style, color, logo, intro&outro and more.

![Team workspace](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6388604483b03a9ecb34d695/684c305996ac160131ce654f_Team%20workspace.avif)

### Team workspace

Easily set up a team account to collaborate and manage creative projects with your team members.

![Workflow integration](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/6388604483b03a9ecb34d695/684c3059b3eecf81e4af57dc_Workflow%20integration.avif)

### Workflow integration

With our API, you can integrate OpusClip with your CMS and other tools to automate your video creation workflow.

## Got questions?

### How does OpusClip work?

OpusClip leverages big data to analyze your video content in relation to the latest social and marketing trends from major platforms, and generates a comprehensive understanding of your video for a data-driven decision on content repurposing. It then picks the highlighting moments of your long video, rearranges them into a viral-worthy short and polishes it with dynamic captions, AI-relayout, smooth transition to ensure that the clip is coherent and attention-grabbing, and ends with a strong call-to-action. [Learn more](https://www.opus.pro/how-does-opus-clip-work)

### What types of videos can I upload?

You can use OpusClip to clip any video type that you have with our newest model [ClipAnything](https://www.opus.pro/clipanything). Whether it's talking-head videos like podcasts and interviews, vlogs, sports, TV shows, or videos with little to no dialogue, ClipAnything understands all the visual, audio and sentiment cues throughout the video, and can clip the best moments from your video. You can also use natural language prompts to clip a specific moment. To learn more about it, please visit the [ClipAnything](https://www.opus.pro/clipanything) page.

### Which languages are supported?

We support English, German, Spanish, French, Portuguese, Italian, Dutch, Russian, Polish, Indonesian, Ukrainian, Swedish, Turkish, Norwegian, Croatian, Romanian, Slovak, Greek, Danish, Finnish, Hungarian, Czech, Japanese, Korean, Vietnamese and more to come.

### Can I add captions?

Absolutely! In fact, OpusClip automatically adds captions for you with over 97% accuracy! You can change text and edit it freely.

### Is OpusClip free to use?

OpusClip is free to use.

If you are a new user, you will enjoy a 7-day free trial of our Pro Plan, which gives you 90 minutes of video processing time (~30 downloadable clips).

Once your free trial ends, you can either upgrade to paid subscription, or use our free-forever plan with 60 minutes of video processing time refreshed monthly.

We offer paid subscription plans with flexible upload credits, available on both a monthly and yearly basis. Please check out further details above.

### I have more questions!

Please join our [Discord](https://discord.com/invite/wqbb7ZKhjg) or email us at [contact@opus.pro](mailto:contact@opus.pro?subject=Questions%20about%20OpusClip) if you need help or have any questions or advice for us.

## Our Values

### Be impossible to ignore

With QuickReel (platform + API), you can turn existing content into hundreds of ready-to-post clips, so posting on socials becomes routine and growth becomes inevitable.

### Every Clip should tell a story

Most clips fail because they're just "cut downs" That's why QuickReel makes sure to edit videos with intent - B-roll, music, and trendy subtitles that make clips engaging and potentially viral.

### Distribution is the new Oil

One platform isn't enough anymore. It's essential to be omnipresent, to be present on all major socials with new & refreshing content. QuickReel connects your socials, generates fresh variants, and auto-schedules across platforms so you find your audience

AI Editing Models

## Meet the AI models behind every viral clip

AI models that understand your video end-to-end. Built for speed, accuracy, and creator-level polish.

![Director model](https://quickreel.io/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.quickreel.io%2Ffe-assets%2Flanding%2Fdirector_model.webp&w=1920&q=75)

### Director model

Finds the most clip-worthy moments automatically. It detects hooks, punchlines, and high-retention segments to generate multiple clips in seconds.

### Reframe model

Auto tracks the speaker and reframes perfectly for 16:9, 1:1, 9:16. Every clip looks native on Shorts/Reels/TikTok.

AI Editing

## AI that edits with you, not just for you

Our AI editing assistant works hand-in-hand with you to refine clips, add effects, and optimize your content.

![AI editor demo](https://quickreel.io/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.quickreel.io%2Ffe-assets%2Flanding%2Feditor_1.webp&w=1920&q=75)

Quickreel for team

## Scale your content output without scaling your team

Short-form is a volume game. QuickReel helps your team create, manage, and publish consistent content at speed.

![Brand templates](https://quickreel.io/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.quickreel.io%2Ffe-assets%2Flanding%2Fbrand_template.webp&w=1920&q=75)

### Brand templates

Create on-brand styles with your fonts, colors, logo, captions, and overlays. Apply them to every clip in one click.

![Team workspace](https://quickreel.io/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.quickreel.io%2Ffe-assets%2Flanding%2Fworkspace.png&w=1920&q=75)

### Team workspace

Organize projects, collaborate with your team, and keep your entire workflow in one shared workspace.

![API integration](https://quickreel.io/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.quickreel.io%2Ffe-assets%2Flanding%2Fquickreel_api.webp&w=1920&q=75)

### API integration

Plug QuickReel into your existing stack with API and automations. Generate clips at scale and push them wherever your team works.

## Beyond AI clipping

Faceless videos, AI images, and voice generation. All inside QuickReel.

### Faceless video generation

Create full videos from a simple prompt. Get scripts, visuals, scenes, captions, and ready-to-post edits without filming.

![Image generation](https://quickreel.io/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.quickreel.io%2Ffe-assets%2Flanding%2Fimage_generation.webp&w=1920&q=75)

### Image generation

Generate high-quality visuals, thumbnails, and post graphics in your style. Perfect for covers, backgrounds, and storytelling frames.

![Voice generation](https://quickreel.io/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.quickreel.io%2Ffe-assets%2Flanding%2Faudio_generation.webp&w=1920&q=75)

### Voice generation

Create lifelike voiceovers in seconds. Pick a voice, set the tone, and generate narration that sounds natural.

## Frequently Asked Questions

Is vidyo.ai now quso.ai?

Yes, [vidyo.ai](https://vidyo.ai/) is now a part of [quso.ai](https://quso.ai/). While [vidyo.ai](https://vidyo.ai/) focused primarily on ai video editing and ai clipping along with social media management, [quso.ai](https://quso.ai/) has expanded into a complete Social Media AI suite. We now offer suite of tools for content creation, scheduling, analytics, and video editing, making it an all-in-one solution for managing your social media presence.

Can I use quso.ai for free?

Yes, quso.ai offers a free trial with limited credits to experience the tool and help you make a better decision.

How does quso.ai work?

quso.ai is an all-in-one Social Media AI marketing platform that simplifies social media management. It helps you create content, manage multiple platforms, and edit videos effortlessly with video AI tools. From generating AI clips, blogs, shownotes, auto-subtitles and social media scheduling, quso.ai automates your workflow to save time and boosts your social media reach.

Who should be using quso.ai?

quso.ai is a Social Media AI platform that helps you increase your reach on social media. Built for coaches, educators, podcasters, business owners and video content creators, quso.ai helps with ai video repurposing and social media scheduling.

I am a beginner, can I use quso.ai?

quso.ai is known for its user-friendly interface, especially for newcomers to AI technology. The software has an intuitive workflow, making it easy for beginners to navigate.

What types of videos can I upload on the quso.ai app?

quso.ai lets you import a video from [YouTube](https://vidyo.ai/templates/youtube-templates) or upload a full video in mp4, m4v, mov & webm format. Free users can upload 5GB and paid users can upload 15GB files.

What languages are supported by quso.ai?

quso.ai currently supports English, Spanish, German, and French and will soon be adding more languages to cater to a wider audience.

Do you have stock video and audio?

Yes, quso.ai has an integrated [B rolls library.](https://quso.ai/products/b-rolls-library) You can enhance your storytelling with our royalty-free stock images, videos and audios.

## Frequently Asked Questions?

I need extra credits, how do I top-up?

The top-up feature is currently exclusive to all paid plans. To add extra credits, simply click on the credit balance on your home screen or use the "Upgrade" tab. From there, you can select your preferred plan to add more credits to your account. It's that easy!

How to upgrade my account/subscription to a Paid Plan?

To upgrade your account, go to your account settings and look for the "Upgrade" button. From there, you'll be able to choose between monthly or annual plans for either option.

Select the plan that suits your needs and follow the prompts to complete the upgrade process.

‍

How to cancel my subscription?

To cancel your subscription, simply navigate to "Settings" in your account settings and then go to the "Billing and Plans" tab. Click on the three dots under your current plan section, and then click "Cancel."

Can I download my invoices?

Yes, under the settings tab, you can now download/view your invoices with just three clicks!

‍

## Frequently asked questions

Can’t find the answer you’re looking for?
Reach out to our customer support team.

### Basics

What is Restream?

Restream is a complete live streaming solution that allows you stream from one place to 30+ social channels.

How do I get started?

Register on our website, connect platform accounts and go live in seconds right from your browser (no setup needed) or your favorite streaming tool. [Learn more](https://support.restream.io/en/articles/8540516-go-live-with-studio-2-0)

Does Restream affect my video quality?

No, Restream doesn't affect your video quality thanks to our innovative technology.

### Pricing

Can I stream for free?

Yes, you can choose 2 from 30+ social channels to multistream for free. Our paid plans offer extra channels and more robust features.

Which plan should I choose?

Our plans are based on the number of channels you need to stream to and additional features. Our support team can help you pick the plan that fits your needs.

What is custom RTMP?

Custom RTMP is a way to stream to a platform that is not listed among our [supported services](https://support.restream.io/en/articles/872029-supported-social-platforms), but provides an RTMP URL and stream key.

### Streaming

Can I stream in full HD?

With our Professional plan, you can stream in 1080p using Restream Studio. If using custom software, there's no restriction, however some platforms may not support Full HD.

Can I stream with stereo sound?

Yes, Restream Studio supports stereo sound.

Can I stream using streaming software?

Yes, you can use any 3rd party streaming software or our intuitive web-based Restream Studio. [Learn more](https://support.restream.io/en/articles/2411868-select-your-streaming-software)

### Features

Can I invite guests to the stream?

Yes, you can add guests with an invite link. Restream supports up to 10 participants. [Learn more](https://support.restream.io/en/articles/8540529-how-to-invite-guests-in-studio)

Can I stream pre-recorded videos?

Yes, you can stream pre-recorded content live with Upload & Stream. [Learn more](https://support.restream.io/en/articles/2715850-schedule-your-video-as-a-pre-recorded-event)

Can I stream to my server or custom destinations?

Yes, you can use our Custom RTMP feature and stream to any custom platform that provides an RTMP URL and stream key. [Learn more](https://support.restream.io/en/articles/369436-stream-to-a-custom-rtmp-channel)

### Resources

Do I need additional bandwidth to multistream?

No, you don't need additional bandwidth to use Restream even if you stream to 30 destinations at once.

Do you have any bitrate limits?

No, Restream doesnt’t have any bitrate limits. Note, that sometimes platforms set their bitrate limits.

Does Restream add any delay?

Any additional delay experienced during streaming is always under 2 seconds. This slight lag can occur occasionally, and the number of channels you're using won't impact it.

### Customisation

Can I switch between cameras and audio sources?

Yes, you can switch between cameras and microphones with a click.

Can I customise my stream?

Yes, Restream offers a rich collection of themes, overlays, logos, and backgrounds for any occasion. Also, you can brand your stream with your own graphics. [Learn more](https://support.restream.io/en/articles/8540835-add-graphics-to-your-stream-in-studio)

Can I stream audio only?

Yes, you can. You can start a live stream with a static image or black screen and broadcast your audio content.

## Why Choose Swiftia for AI Clip Solutions

Struggling to keep up with the demand for short-form video? Traditional editing tools are slow, expensive, and require expert skills.

Effortlessly convert your webinars, podcasts, and long-form videos into captivating shorts optimized for maximum engagement.

Our advanced API streamlines AI clips generation and repurposing for businesses and content creators, facilitating seamless sharing across various online platforms.

## AI-Powered Features to Transform Your Video Marketing.

##### Swiftia's features

##### Caption Animation Engine

Enhance viewer engagement and retention by leveraging our sophisticated Caption Animation Engine, offering a diverse range of animations to optimize watch time.

05-video

##### Filler Word Removal Algorithm

Employ our advanced Filler Word Removal Algorithm to automatically eliminate extraneous filler words, ensuring a pristine and polished audio output for your videos.

06-video

##### Up to 4K Resolution Support

Elevate your visual content with Swiftia's API, supporting resolutions up to 4K to guarantee impeccable video quality and clarity for a superior viewing experience.

07-scipt

##### Multi-language Integration

## FAQ

How do I upgrade from the free plan to the paid plan?

You can upgrade to the paid plan directly from your workspace or clicking ‘Upgrade’ button. Simply select the plan that suits you and follow the prompts to complete the upgrade process.

Can I change or cancel my plan at any time?

Yes, you can change or cancel your plan at any time by accessing your account settings. Once you cancel, the plan will expire at the end of your billing cycle.

What payment methods do you accept?

We accept a variety of payment methods, including credit cards, PayPal, Stripe and bank transfers. You can select your preferred payment method during the checkout process.

What kind of support is available with each plan?

All plans come with basic support via email. The team plan includes priority support, while the custom plan includes dedicated support with a dedicated account manager.

How is payment being processed?

We use Stripe as our payment processor. This means that when you make a payment, all payment details are handled directly by Stripe and Vizard does not have access to your credit card data.

How can I cancel my plan?

You can directly go to “Workspace-Subscription” to find the cancel option for your subscription.

FAQ

## Frequently asked questions

Expand All

1. ### Can I use WayinVideo for free?


Yes, you can. Sign up and you’ll instantly receive 200 free credits to start creating with WayinVideo.

2. ### Can I receive an invoice?


Yes. You can download invoices and receipts as PDFs in the web app under [Settings > Plan > Invoice](https://wayin.ai/wayinvideo/settings/plan).

3. ### Will my subscription plan renew automatically?


Yes. Monthly and yearly subscriptions renew automatically on your billing date unless you cancel before the renewal date.

4. ### What payment methods do you accept?


We support a wide range of major payment methods, including credit cards, debit cards, Apple Pay, Google Pay, Link, and more.

5. ### Can I cancel my subscription at any time?


Yes. To cancel your subscription, go to [Settings > Profile > Current Plan](https://wayin.ai/wayinvideo/settings/plan) and click “Change”. Your subscription benefits will remain active until the end of your current billing cycle, after which your membership will automatically expire. Please note that payments are nonrefundable.

6. ### Do unused credits roll over to the next month?


No. Your credits are automatically reset every month, so unused credits do not roll over to the next billing period.

7. ### How do credits work?


Credits are deducted based on the task performed:

- 1 min video for AI Clipping = **2 credits**
- 1 min video for Find Moments = **2 credits** (first use), **1 credit** (repeated use)
- 1 min video for AI Subtitles = **0.5 credit**
- 1 min video for Video Transcript = **0.5 credit**
- 1 min video for Video Summaries = **1 credit**
- 1 min video for AI Reframe = **0.5 credit**
- 1 Bot Chat Question = **0.2 credit**
- 1 In-Depth Understanding = **0.2 credit**

8. ### Still have questions or feedback?


Join our [Discord community](https://discord.com/invite/xNHGuaKxQ4) to share your thoughts anytime.

## Turn Hours of Editing Into Minutes of Magic

## AI Reframe: AI That Understands Every Pixel

Our AI doesn't just crop—it comprehends. It analyzes every pixel of your video to detect speakers, action, and context, then applies the perfect layout automatically. Split-screen for debates, picture-in-picture for gaming reactions, multi-screen for podcasts. One click resizes for all platforms. Different platforms need different sizes, but you only need one tool.

FAQ

## Frequently asked questions

Expand All

1. ### How do I make video clips for free?


Just upload your video or paste a link into WayinVideo. Our AI clip maker automatically creates multiple viral-ready clips in 30 seconds. You'll receive 200 credits upon signup, plus free daily credits to keep creating—no credit card needed for the initial trial, no watermarks. Ready to post in minutes.

2. ### What is the best free clip maker?


WayinVideo is the best free clip maker with AI-powered viral moment detection, smart reframing, animated captions, and text-based editing. We're faster than traditional clip makers, more generous with free credits, and never add watermarks—even on the free plan.

3. ### How does the AI clip maker work?


Our AI video clipping technology scans your entire video to find the best parts—funny moments, emotional reactions, surprising reveals. As a powerful ai clip generator, it automatically creates short clips optimized for social media, complete with captions and perfect sizing for TikTok, Reels, and Shorts.

4. ### What video formats and lengths are supported?


Videos up to several hours long are supported. Our clip maker supports extra-long videos, even ones over 10 hours long. All major video formats work—MP4, MOV, and more. You can also import directly from YouTube, Facebook, Dailymotion, TikTok, Twitch, and Vimeo to clip video online. No need to download video clipping software—everything works in your browser. Note that credits are calculated based on video length.

5. ### Do you add watermarks to clips?


Never. No watermarks, not even on free clips. Your clips stay clean and 100% yours. Post them anywhere, look professional.

6. ### How many clips can I create from one video?


Typically 8-15 clips from a 20-minute video. The exact number depends on your video's total length and how many highlight moments it contains. Videos with lots of action or talking points may generate even more clips.

7. ### Can I also generate AI videos from text?


Yes! Beyond clipping existing videos, WayinVideo also offers a full AI video generator. Create original videos from text prompts or animate images using top models like Sora, Veo, and Wan—all in one platform. You can also generate AI Hook intros (headlines + voiceover) and AI B-roll images to fill your timeline faster.
